08/07/2022, 10:15 am - Devyansh: #include <stdio.h>
void binarysearch(int[], int);
int main()
{
	int n, arr[n], i;
	printf("enter no of no. you want to enter in array");
	scanf("%d", &n);
	for(i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		printf("enter %d no ", (i+1));
		scanf("%d", &arr[i]);
	}
	printf("entered array is\n");
	for(i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		printf("\nentered no is %d , %d", (i+1), arr[i]);
	}
	binarysearch(arr, n);
}
void binarysearch(int arr[],int n)
{
	int mid, end=n, st=0, i, f, j=0;
	printf("\nenter the number you want to find ");
	scanf("%d", &f);	
	for(i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		mid=(st+end)/2;
		if(arr[mid]==f)
		{
			printf("\n%d number found at position %d ", f, (mid+1));
			j=1;
			break;
		}
		else if(f>arr[mid])
		{
			st=mid;
		}
		else
		{
			end=mid;
		}
	}
}

24/09/2022, 1:26 pm - Ayush Choudhary: NASA International Space Apps Challenge is NASA's annual global hackathon. It will be a *24-hour coding + non-coding competition* as per the challenges. You will be given some challenges (available at the website) and you have to create a project for the same. 

Galgotias will be the only one in the entire Delhi NCR belt to host Space Apps. The event will take place worldwide on *October 1 & 2*. Winners will be awarded at galgotias as well as will be nominated for Global judging.

Galgotias hosted Space Apps last in 2019. That year it was 150+ teams from 20+ colleges and 5+ states in our campus.

*Types of challenges* include creation of Websites, Mobile applications, Engaging Videos, AI-ML products, etc. Teams will get access to data from NASA and other space agencies like ISRO for completing their challenges. 

Team size should be *2-6 members* per team. You have to register individually as of now and then await further instructions related to participation.

For more info, refer: bit.ly/nasa-space-apps-gn

17/11/2022, 3:01 pm - Asheesh: Hello✨
Our juniors of DCRUST.
We Lisocians are here!

LISOC is the literary society of DCRUST Murthal, Sonepat that has been active in the domain of literature and oration for the past 20 years.
📌‌The motto of our society is LIVE WORK PLAY. 
‌We aim to inculcate a sense of professionalism in an individual through various drills. 
📌‌We balance each and every aspect of literature from oration to creative writing. Reading is a paramount requisite in augmenting growth. Therefore, a book is read by each member every month and its review is written alongside.
📌‌Our members get a chance to augment themselves with management skills as they organize and coordinate various events under the guidance of seniors. 
📌‌We work well to publish a wall magazine every semester, popularly known as the VOX POPULI. Vox Populi is a theme based wall magazine with the meaning of THE VOICE OF PEOPLE.
📌‌We have not just touched the sky of DCRUST, but have lived a lot of sunrises at various other institutions like IIM Rohtak, IIT Delhi, NIT Kurukshetra and the list goes on.
LISOC is more than an organisation. It is a family that works day and night to intensify the love for literature in people and pique their interest in such campaigns. We are a team that makes better goals than the previous ones and leaves no stone unturned in accomplishing them only to look back at them and smile.

 _From ordinary to extraordinary_ 

 The official event management and personality development society of dcrust 
Presents you *"IDEA* *CHALLENGE"* and *"RIDDLE HUNTER"* under *TECHNOVA 2022* 

 💡*IDEA CHALLENGE*💡 

 _" to make ideas a reality, we must act, experiment, fail, adapt, and learn on a daily basis."_ 
DAY  🌅   :- *THURSDAY* 
DATE 📅  :- *15th December 2022* 
TIME  🕒 :- *2:00 PM -5:00 PM* 
VENUE :- *MV 312* 

 *Idea challenge* - a innovative and creative event to enhance the intellectual capabilities of an individual which will help to think out of the box.
 It consists of three rounds as follows :

 *ROUND 1* 

In this round a set of questions will be asked from various teams and the teams who will give most innovative answers will be chosen for next rounds.

 *Round 2* 

 _"Difficulties don't come to destroy you , but to   make you realize your hidden potential"_ 

This round will be a level up, selected  participants will again answer some more difficult questions.The most innovative and creative answers will be chosen for next round. 

 *ROUND 3* 

IN this round team members have to prepare a report on any one of the theme which will be given to them on the spot and give a verbal presentation of the same.

 *RIDDLE HUNTER* 

Day🌅   :- *FRIDAY* 
Date  📅 :- *16th December 2022* 
Time   🕒:- *9:00 AM - 2:00 PM* 
Venue  :- *lawn near main stage* 

 _"All is a riddle and key to a riddle is another riddle"_ 

This event will have two rounds as follows:-

 *Round 1* 

In this round the team members have to guess the riddles and teams which will give the right answers in minimal time will be chosen for next round.

 *Round 2* 

Round 2 is a fun event called as *"TREASURE* *HUNT"* in which teams will be given different clues and from those clues they will have yo reach to the final location where they'll find treasure.

03/06/2023, 7:22 pm - +91 95186 69614: Hi Guys,
Here is some info for all to consider while selecting electives.

There needs to be a minimum majority among us to get the subjects we want .
As per discussion with seniors, last year mostly took software engineering as elective but this time that's kept as our main subject,
Also last year, programming languages and introduction to data science were offered. So we have a good prob this year too for these two subjects.

Recommendations u may consider :
Those who want to go for CAT in future, recommendation is to go for Data Science due to business analytics and stuff that's related.
Those who want to go for gate, recommended subject is programming languages as that would be easier to pursue.  

But one fact is, in coming semesters there is no continuation of programming languages subjects but there is continuation for data science elective 
6th sem, data analytics is there as an option for electives 

Also, there is no impact of specialisation on placement as the scenario will be if u have knowledge then it won't matter if it came from specialisation or your self study.(Not opposing people who are taking specialisation, i got this query so here's the answer) u just need to have relevant knowledge.

These were the facts that i could gather, you can think and choose your subjects wisely.

All the best👍🏻

22/09/2023, 11:06 pm - Ayush Choudhary: To
The  Vice Chancellor 
DCRUST Murthal 

*Subject :- Requesting for AMBULANCE service in university campus *

Sir,
I am writing to you to bring your attention towards the matter that currently we don’t have a ambulance inside our university campus.

As you may know, the campus is located in semi urban area, and it can take a significant amount of time for an ambulance to arrive from a nearby city. This can be life-threatening in the event of a medical emergency.

Recently, a student dislocated his knee while playing volleyball in the hostel. It took almost 45 minutes for an ambulance to arrive, which caused the student unnecessary pain and suffering.

I understand that providing an ambulance service on campus is a significant investment, but I believe that it is a worthwhile one. The safety and well-being of our students should be our top priority.

An ambulance service on campus would provide students with peace of mind knowing that they would have immediate access to medical care in the event of an emergency. It would also reduce the amount of time that students have to wait for an ambulance.

I urge you to consider my request and to take steps to provide an ambulance service in the DCRUST Murthal campus.

Thank you for your time and consideration.

Sincerely,
Students of DCRUST Murthal

23/10/2023, 11:26 pm - Asheesh: 📜 *Unlock the Epic World of Ramayana with LISOC - The Official Literary Society of DCRUST Murthal! 🪔🏹*

📖 *Ramayana Connect: Where Legendary Tales Unite!* 📜

Prepare for an extraordinary journey this Dussehra as we unveil "Ramayana Connect," a literary event that bridges the past and present, the fictional and the tangible.

🌟 *How it Works:*

1️⃣ Dive into the awe-inspiring world of The Ramayana. Choose two iconic characters from our list of legends, including Lord Rama, Sita, Ravan, Hanuman, and many more! 📜

2️⃣ In this unique event, participants must select two characters from the given options. Then, you'll step into the shoes of one character and write a letter from their perspective to the other character. Pour out your compliments, suggestions, or express your heartfelt grievances in 100-120 words, just like the epic itself! ✍🗯

3️⃣ Let your words craft history! The most riveting letter will be crowned the winner, and the author shall receive a grand reward! 🏆

*Why Participate:*

🧡 Immerse yourself in the timeless epic of Ramayana.
🖋 Sharpen your creative writing prowess.
🏆 Win fabulous prizes and literary acclaim.
🌟 Connect with fellow wordsmiths and literature aficionados.
🤝 Showcase your literary brilliance to the world.
